The core architecture consists of:\\n\\n**Abstract Interface and Validation Results:**\\n- `source/common/tls/cert_validator/cert_validator.h` defines the abstract `CertValidator` interface with methods for `doVerifyCertChain()`, `addClientValidationContext()`, and `initializeSslContexts()`. It handles X.509 certificate chain verification using OpenSSL/BoringSSL APIs. Key methods include:\\n  - `doVerifyCertChain()`: Verifies the complete certificate chain\\n  - `verifyCertificate()`: Validates individual X.509 certificates\\n  - `verifyCertificateHashList()` and `verifyCertificateSpkiList()`: Pin verification against certificate hashes and SPKI values\\n  - `matchSubjectAltName()` and `verifySubjectAltName()`: SAN matching logic\\n\\n**Subject Alternative Name (SAN) Matcher:**\\n- `source/common/tls/cert_validator/san_matcher.h` and `san_matcher.cc` provide the `SanMatcher` interface and `StringSanMatcher` implementation. The matcher supports multiple SAN types:\\n  - DNS names (GEN_DNS)\\n  - URIs (GEN_URI)\\n  - Email addresses (GEN_EMAIL)\\n  - IP addresses (GEN_IPADD)\\n  - Other names with specific OIDs (GEN_OTHERNAME)\\n- The `createStringSanMatcher()` factory function creates type-specific matchers based on the `SubjectAltNameMatcher` configuration.\\n\\n**TLS Context Management:**\\n- `source/common/tls/context_impl.h` and `context_impl.cc` define `ContextImpl` which manages TLS certificates and the associated `cert_validator_` instance. The `TlsContext` struct holds OpenSSL SSL_CTX and certificate data.\\n- `source/common/tls/server_context_impl.h` and `server_context_impl.cc` extend ContextImpl with server-specific functionality including:\\n  - `selectTlsContext()`: Selects appropriate TLS context based on ClientHello\\n  - `findTlsContext()`: Locates the right certificate context and manages OCSP stapling decisions\\n- `source/common/tls/client_context_impl.h` and `client_context_impl.cc` provide client-side TLS context functionality.\\n\\n**OCSP Response Parsing and Stapling Support:**\\n- `source/common/tls/ocsp/ocsp.h` and `ocsp.cc` define structures for OCSP response handling:\\n  - `OcspResponse`: Top-level response structure with status and response data\\n  - `OcspResponseStatus`: Enumeration of possible OCSP response statuses (Successful, MalformedRequest, InternalError, etc.)\\n  - `BasicOcspResponse`: Implementation of the BasicOCSPResponse from RFC 6960\\n  - `SingleResponse`: Individual certificate status response with this_update_ and next_update_ timestamps\\n  - `ResponseData` and `CertId`: Supporting structures for tracking certificate validity\\n- `source/common/tls/ocsp/asn1_utility.h` and `asn1_utility.cc` provide low-level ASN.1 parsing utilities for extracting OCSP response data.\\n- OCSP stapling is integrated into `ServerContextImpl` with staple policy enforcement (LENIENT_STAPLING, STRICT_STAPLING, MUST_STAPLE) and runtime decisions about when to include OCSP responses in TLS handshakes.\\n\\n**Factory Pattern:**\\n- `source/common/tls/cert_validator/factory.h` and `factory.cc` define `CertValidatorFactory` for creating validator instances.
